### File 9: gradlew
**Path:** `android\gradlew`
**Size:** 4.85 KB

```text
#!/usr/bin/env bash

##############################################################################
##
##  Gradle start up script for UN*X
##
##############################################################################

# Add default JVM options here. You can also use JAVA_OPTS and GRADLE_OPTS to pass JVM options to this script.
DEFAULT_JVM_OPTS=""

APP_NAME="Gradle"
APP_BASE_NAME=`basename "$0"`

# Use the maximum available, or set MAX_FD != -1 to use that value.
MAX_FD="maximum"

warn ( ) {
    echo "$*"
}

die ( ) {
    echo
    echo "$*"
    echo
    exit 1
}

# OS specific support (must be 'true' or 'false').
cygwin=false
msys=false
darwin=false
case "`uname`" in
  CYGWIN* )
    cygwin=true
    ;;
  Darwin* )
    darwin=true
    ;;
  MINGW* )
    msys=true
    ;;
esac

# Attempt to set APP_HOME
# Resolve links: $0 may be a link
PRG="$0"
# Need this for relative symlinks.
while [ -h "$PRG" ] ; do
    ls=`ls -ld "$PRG"`
    link=`expr "$ls" : '.*-> \(.*\)$'`
    if expr "$link" : '/.*' > /dev/null; then
        PRG="$link"
    else
        PRG=`dirname "$PRG"`"/$link"
    fi
done
SAVED="`pwd`"
cd "`dirname \"$PRG\"`/" >/dev/null
APP_HOME="`pwd -P`"
cd "$SAVED" >/dev/null

CLASSPATH=$APP_HOME/gradle/wrapper/gradle-wrapper.jar

# Determine the Java command to use to start the JVM.
if [ -n "$JAVA_HOME" ] ; then
    if [ -x "$JAVA_HOME/jre/sh/java" ] ; then
        # IBM's JDK on AIX uses strange locations for the executables
        JAVACMD="$JAVA_HOME/jre/sh/java"
    else
        JAVACMD="$JAVA_HOME/bin/java"
    fi
    if [ ! -x "$JAVACMD" ] ; then
        die "ERROR: JAVA_HOME is set to an invalid directory: $JAVA_HOME

Please set the JAVA_HOME variable in your environment to match the
location of your Java installation."
    fi
else
    JAVACMD="java"
    which java >/dev/null 2>&1 || die "ERROR: JAVA_HOME is not set and no 'java' command could be found in your PATH.

Please set the JAVA_HOME variable in your environment to match the
location of your Java installation."
fi

# Increase the maximum file descriptors if we can.
if [ "$cygwin" = "false" -a "$darwin" = "false" ] ; then
    MAX_FD_LIMIT=`ulimit -H -n`
    if [ $? -eq 0 ] ; then
        if [ "$MAX_FD" = "maximum" -o "$MAX_FD" = "max" ] ; then
            MAX_FD="$MAX_FD_LIMIT"
        fi
        ulimit -n $MAX_FD
        if [ $? -ne 0 ] ; then
            warn "Could not set maximum file descriptor limit: $MAX_FD"
        fi
    else
        warn "Could not query maximum file descriptor limit: $MAX_FD_LIMIT"
    fi
fi

# For Darwin, add options to specify how the application appears in the dock
if $darwin; then
    GRADLE_OPTS="$GRADLE_OPTS \"-Xdock:name=$APP_NAME\" \"-Xdock:icon=$APP_HOME/media/gradle.icns\""
fi

# For Cygwin, switch paths to Windows format before running java
if $cygwin ; then
    APP_HOME=`cygpath --path --mixed "$APP_HOME"`
    CLASSPATH=`cygpath --path --mixed "$CLASSPATH"`
    JAVACMD=`cygpath --unix "$JAVACMD"`

    # We build the pattern for arguments to be converted via cygpath
    ROOTDIRSRAW=`find -L / -maxdepth 1 -mindepth 1 -type d 2>/dev/null`
    SEP=""
    for dir in $ROOTDIRSRAW ; do
        ROOTDIRS="$ROOTDIRS$SEP$dir"
        SEP="|"
    done
    OURCYGPATTERN="(^($ROOTDIRS))"
    # Add a user-defined pattern to the cygpath arguments
    if [ "$GRADLE_CYGPATTERN" != "" ] ; then
        OURCYGPATTERN="$OURCYGPATTERN|($GRADLE_CYGPATTERN)"
    fi
    # Now convert the arguments - kludge to limit ourselves to /bin/sh
    i=0
    for arg in "$@" ; do
        CHECK=`echo "$arg"|egrep -c "$OURCYGPATTERN" -`
        CHECK2=`echo "$arg"|egrep -c "^-"`                                 ### Determine if an option

        if [ $CHECK -ne 0 ] && [ $CHECK2 -eq 0 ] ; then                    ### Added a condition
            eval `echo args$i`=`cygpath --path --ignore --mixed "$arg"`
        else
            eval `echo args$i`="\"$arg\""
        fi
        i=$((i+1))
    done
    case $i in
        (0) set -- ;;
        (1) set -- "$args0" ;;
        (2) set -- "$args0" "$args1" ;;
        (3) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" ;;
        (4) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" ;;
        (5) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" ;;
        (6) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" "$args5" ;;
        (7) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" "$args5" "$args6" ;;
        (8) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" "$args5" "$args6" "$args7" ;;
        (9) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" "$args5" "$args6" "$args7" "$args8" ;;
    esac
fi

# Split up the JVM_OPTS And GRADLE_OPTS values into an array, following the shell quoting and substitution rules
function splitJvmOpts() {
    JVM_OPTS=("$@")
}
eval splitJvmOpts $DEFAULT_JVM_OPTS $JAVA_OPTS $GRADLE_OPTS
JVM_OPTS[${#JVM_OPTS[*]}]="-Dorg.gradle.appname=$APP_BASE_NAME"

exec "$JAVACMD" "${JVM_OPTS[@]}" -classpath "$CLASSPATH" org.gradle.wrapper.GradleWrapperMain "$@"

```

### File 10: gradlew.bat
**Path:** `android\gradlew.bat`
**Size:** 2.35 KB

```text
@if "%DEBUG%" == "" @echo off
@rem ##########################################################################
@rem
@rem  Gradle startup script for Windows
@rem
@rem ##########################################################################

@rem Set local scope for the variables with windows NT shell
if "%OS%"=="Windows_NT" setlocal

@rem Add default JVM options here. You can also use JAVA_OPTS and GRADLE_OPTS to pass JVM options to this script.
set DEFAULT_JVM_OPTS=

set DIRNAME=%~dp0
if "%DIRNAME%" == "" set DIRNAME=.
set APP_BASE_NAME=%~n0
set APP_HOME=%DIRNAME%

@rem Find java.exe
if defined JAVA_HOME goto findJavaFromJavaHome

set JAVA_EXE=java.exe
%JAVA_EXE% -version >NUL 2>&1
if "%ERRORLEVEL%" == "0" goto init

echo.
echo ERROR: JAVA_HOME is not set and no 'java' command could be found in your PATH.
echo.
echo Please set the JAVA_HOME variable in your environment to match the
echo location of your Java installation.

goto fail

:findJavaFromJavaHome
set JAVA_HOME=%JAVA_HOME:"=%
set JAVA_EXE=%JAVA_HOME%/bin/java.exe

if exist "%JAVA_EXE%" goto init

echo.
echo ERROR: JAVA_HOME is set to an invalid directory: %JAVA_HOME%
echo.
echo Please set the JAVA_HOME variable in your environment to match the
echo location of your Java installation.

goto fail

:init
@rem Get command-line arguments, handling Windowz variants

if not "%OS%" == "Windows_NT" goto win9xME_args
if "%@eval[2+2]" == "4" goto 4NT_args

:win9xME_args
@rem Slurp the command line arguments.
set CMD_LINE_ARGS=
set _SKIP=2

:win9xME_args_slurp
if "x%~1" == "x" goto execute

set CMD_LINE_ARGS=%*
goto execute

:4NT_args
@rem Get arguments from the 4NT Shell from JP Software
set CMD_LINE_ARGS=%$

:execute
@rem Setup the command line

set CLASSPATH=%APP_HOME%\gradle\wrapper\gradle-wrapper.jar

@rem Execute Gradle
"%JAVA_EXE%" %DEFAULT_JVM_OPTS% %JAVA_OPTS% %GRADLE_OPTS% "-Dorg.gradle.appname=%APP_BASE_NAME%" -classpath "%CLASSPATH%" org.gradle.wrapper.GradleWrapperMain %CMD_LINE_ARGS%

:end
@rem End local scope for the variables with windows NT shell
if "%ERRORLEVEL%"=="0" goto mainEnd

:fail
rem Set variable GRADLE_EXIT_CONSOLE if you need the _script_ return code instead of
rem the _cmd.exe /c_ return code!
if  not "" == "%GRADLE_EXIT_CONSOLE%" exit 1
exit /b 1

:mainEnd
if "%OS%"=="Windows_NT" endlocal

:omega

```

```dart
class SpendlyApp extends StatelessWidget {
```

### File 27: csv_exporter.dart
**Path:** `lib\helpers\csv_exporter.dart`
**Size:** 3.45 KB

```dart
import 'dart:io';
import 'package:path_provider/path_provider.dart';
import 'package:intl/intl.dart';
import '../models/transaction.dart';

class CsvExporter {
  // Generate CSV content from transactions
  static String generateCsv(List<Transaction> transactions) {
    final buffer = StringBuffer();

    // Header
    buffer.writeln('Date,Merchant,Amount,Category,Type');

    // Data rows
    for (var transaction in transactions) {
      final date = DateFormat('yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm').format(transaction.dateTime);
      final merchant = _escapeCsv(transaction.merchantName);
      final amount = transaction.amount.toStringAsFixed(2);
      final category = transaction.category;
      final type = transaction.isDebit ? 'Debit' : 'Credit';

      buffer.writeln('$date,$merchant,$amount,$category,$type');
    }

    return buffer.toString();
  }

  // Escape CSV special characters
  static String _escapeCsv(String value) {
    if (value.contains(',') || value.contains('"') || value.contains('\n')) {
      return '"${value.replaceAll('"', '""')}"';
    }
    return value;
  }

  // Save CSV to file
  static Future<File> saveCsv(List<Transaction> transactions) async {
    final csv = generateCsv(transactions);

    // Get downloads directory
    Directory? directory;
    if (Platform.isAndroid) {
      directory = Directory('/storage/emulated/0/Download');
      if (!await directory.exists()) {
        directory = await getExternalStorageDirectory();
      }
    } else {
      directory = await getApplicationDocumentsDirectory();
    }

    // Generate filename with timestamp
    final timestamp = DateFormat('yyyyMMdd_HHmmss').format(DateTime.now());
    final filename = 'spendly_transactions_$timestamp.csv';

    // Save file
    final file = File('${directory!.path}/$filename');
    await file.writeAsString(csv);

    return file;
  }

  // Generate monthly summary
  static String generateMonthlySummary(List<Transaction> transactions) {
    final now = DateTime.now();
    final thisMonth = transactions.where((t) =>
    t.dateTime.year == now.year && t.dateTime.month == now.month
    ).toList();

    final totalSpent = thisMonth
        .where((t) => t.isDebit)
        .fold<double>(0.0, (sum, t) => sum + t.amount);

    final totalReceived = thisMonth
        .where((t) => !t.isDebit)
        .fold<double>(0.0, (sum, t) => sum + t.amount);

    // Category breakdown
    final categoryMap = <String, double>{};
    for (var t in thisMonth.where((t) => t.isDebit)) {
      categoryMap[t.category] = (categoryMap[t.category] ?? 0.0) + t.amount;
    }

    final buffer = StringBuffer();
    buffer.writeln('=== Monthly Summary ===\n');
    buffer.writeln('Month: ${DateFormat('MMMM yyyy').format(now)}');
    buffer.writeln('Total Transactions: ${thisMonth.length}');
    buffer.writeln('Total Spent: â‚¹${totalSpent.toStringAsFixed(2)}');
    buffer.writeln('Total Received: â‚¹${totalReceived.toStringAsFixed(2)}');
    buffer.writeln('Net: â‚¹${(totalReceived - totalSpent).toStringAsFixed(2)}');
    buffer.writeln('\n=== Category Breakdown ===\n');

    final sorted = categoryMap.entries.toList()
      ..sort((a, b) => b.value.compareTo(a.value));

    for (var entry in sorted) {
      final percentage = (entry.value / totalSpent * 100).toStringAsFixed(1);
      buffer.writeln('${entry.key}: â‚¹${entry.value.toStringAsFixed(2)} ($percentage%)');
    }

    return buffer.toString();
  }
}
```

### File 28: sms_permission_helper.dart
**Path:** `lib\helpers\sms_permission_helper.dart`
**Size:** 1.15 KB

```dart
import 'package:permission_handler/permission_handler.dart';

class SmsPermissionHelper {
  /// Check if SMS permission is granted
  static Future<bool> isPermissionGranted() async {
    final status = await Permission.sms.status;
    return status.isGranted;
  }

  /// Request SMS permission
  static Future<PermissionStatus> requestPermission() async {
    final status = await Permission.sms.request();
    return status;
  }

  /// Check if permission is permanently denied
  static Future<bool> isPermanentlyDenied() async {
    final status = await Permission.sms.status;
    return status.isPermanentlyDenied;
  }

  /// Open app settings
  static Future<void> openSettings() async {
    await openAppSettings();
  }

  /// Get detailed permission status
  static Future<Map<String, dynamic>> getPermissionInfo() async {
    final smsStatus = await Permission.sms.status;

    return {
      'sms_granted': smsStatus.isGranted,
      'sms_denied': smsStatus.isDenied,
      'sms_permanently_denied': smsStatus.isPermanentlyDenied,
      'sms_restricted': smsStatus.isRestricted,
      'sms_limited': smsStatus.isLimited,
    };
  }
}
```

### File 29: validation_helper.dart
**Path:** `lib\helpers\validation_helper.dart`
**Size:** 1.11 KB

```dart
class ValidationHelper {
  // Amount validation
  static String? validateAmount(String amount) {
    if (amount.isEmpty || amount == '0' || amount == '0.') {
      return 'Please enter amount';
    }

    final value = double.tryParse(amount);
    if (value == null) {
      return 'Invalid amount';
    }

    if (value <= 0) {
      return 'Amount must be greater than 0';
    }

    if (value > 1000000) {
      return 'Amount too large (max â‚¹10,00,000)';
    }

    return null;
  }

  // Decimal validation
  static bool isValidDecimal(String amount) {
    final parts = amount.split('.');
    if (parts.length > 2) return false;
    if (parts.length == 2 && parts[1].length > 2) return false;
    return true;
  }

  // Format amount for display
  static String formatAmount(String amount) {
    if (amount.isEmpty || amount == '0') return '0';

    // Remove leading zeros
    String formatted = amount.replaceFirst(RegExp(r'^0+(?!$)'), '');

    // If starts with . then add 0
    if (formatted.startsWith('.')) {
      formatted = '0$formatted';
    }

    return formatted;
  }
}

```

### File 30: transaction.dart
**Path:** `lib\models\transaction.dart`
**Size:** 1.70 KB

```dart
import 'dart:convert';

class Transaction {
  final String id;
  final String merchantName;
  final double amount;
  final DateTime dateTime;
  final String category;
  final bool isDebit;

  Transaction({
    required this.id,
    required this.merchantName,
    required this.amount,
    required this.dateTime,
    required this.category,
    this.isDebit = true,
  });

  // âœ… NEW: Convert Transaction to JSON (for saving)
  Map<String, dynamic> toJson() {
    return {
      'id': id,
      'merchantName': merchantName,
      'amount': amount,
      'dateTime': dateTime.toIso8601String(),
      'category': category,
      'isDebit': isDebit,
    };
  }

  // âœ… NEW: Create Transaction from JSON (for loading)
  factory Transaction.fromJson(Map<String, dynamic> json) {
    return Transaction(
      id: json['id'] as String,
      merchantName: json['merchantName'] as String,
      amount: (json['amount'] as num).toDouble(),
      dateTime: DateTime.parse(json['dateTime'] as String),
      category: json['category'] as String,
      isDebit: json['isDebit'] as bool,
    );
  }

  // Existing methods (keep as is)
  String get formattedAmount {
    final sign = isDebit ? '-' : '+';
    return '$signâ‚¹${amount.toStringAsFixed(2)}';
  }

  String get formattedTime {
    final now = DateTime.now();
    final diff = now.difference(dateTime);

    if (diff.inDays == 0) {
      return 'Today, ${dateTime.hour}:${dateTime.minute.toString().padLeft(2, '0')}';
    }
    if (diff.inDays == 1) {
      return 'Yesterday, ${dateTime.hour}:${dateTime.minute.toString().padLeft(2, '0')}';
    }
    return '${dateTime.day}/${dateTime.month}/${dateTime.year}';
  }
}

```

### File 31: expense_provider.dart
**Path:** `lib\providers\expense_provider.dart`
**Size:** 4.73 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:shared_preferences/shared_preferences.dart';
import 'dart:convert';
import '../models/transaction.dart';

class ExpenseProvider extends ChangeNotifier {
  List<Transaction> _transactions = [];
  bool _isLoading = true;

  List<Transaction> get transactions => [..._transactions];
  bool get isLoading => _isLoading;

  // Constructor - Load data when provider is created
  ExpenseProvider() {
    loadExpenses();
  }

  // LOAD EXPENSES FROM DISK
  Future<void> loadExpenses() async {
    try {
      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
      final transactionsJson = prefs.getString('transactions');

      if (transactionsJson != null) {
        final List<dynamic> decoded = jsonDecode(transactionsJson);
        _transactions = decoded
            .map((json) => Transaction.fromJson(json as Map<String, dynamic>))
            .toList();
      }
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('Error loading expenses: $e');  // Changed from print
      _transactions = [];
    } finally {
      _isLoading = false;
      notifyListeners();
    }
  }

  // SAVE EXPENSES TO DISK
  Future<void> _saveExpensesToDisk() async {
    try {
      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
      final transactionsJson = _transactions
          .map((transaction) => transaction.toJson())
          .toList();

      await prefs.setString('transactions', jsonEncode(transactionsJson));
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('Error saving expenses: $e');  // Changed from print
    }
  }

  // Total spent calculation (all time)
  double get totalSpent {
    return _transactions
        .where((t) => t.isDebit)
        .fold(0.0, (sum, t) => sum + t.amount);
  }

  // Add expense (with auto-save)
  void addExpense(Transaction transaction) {
    _transactions.insert(0, transaction);
    notifyListeners();
    _saveExpensesToDisk();
  }

  // Delete expense (with auto-save)
  void deleteExpense(String transactionId) {
    _transactions.removeWhere((t) => t.id == transactionId);
    notifyListeners();
    _saveExpensesToDisk();
  }

  // Update expense (with auto-save)
  void updateExpense(Transaction updatedTransaction) {
    final index = _transactions.indexWhere((t) => t.id == updatedTransaction.id);
    if (index != -1) {
      _transactions[index] = updatedTransaction;
      notifyListeners();
      _saveExpensesToDisk();
    }
  }

  // Get recent transactions (last 10)
  List<Transaction> getRecentTransactions() {
    return _transactions.take(10).toList();
  }

  // GET TRANSACTIONS BY PERIOD FILTER LOGIC
  List<Transaction> getTransactionsByPeriod(String period) {
    final now = DateTime.now();

    switch (period) {
      case 'Today':
        return _transactions.where((t) {
          return t.dateTime.year == now.year &&
              t.dateTime.month == now.month &&
              t.dateTime.day == now.day;
        }).toList();

      case 'This Week':
        final weekday = now.weekday == 7 ? 0 : now.weekday;
        final weekStart = now.subtract(Duration(days: weekday));
        final weekStartMidnight = DateTime(weekStart.year, weekStart.month, weekStart.day);
        return _transactions.where((t) {
          return t.dateTime.isAfter(weekStartMidnight.subtract(const Duration(seconds: 1)));
        }).toList();

      case 'This Month':
        return _transactions.where((t) {
          return t.dateTime.year == now.year &&
              t.dateTime.month == now.month;
        }).toList();

      case 'Last Month':
        final lastMonth = now.month == 1
            ? DateTime(now.year - 1, 12)
            : DateTime(now.year, now.month - 1);
        return _transactions.where((t) {
          return t.dateTime.year == lastMonth.year &&
              t.dateTime.month == lastMonth.month;
        }).toList();

      case 'All Time':
        return _transactions;

      default:
        return _transactions;
    }
  }

  // GET TOTAL SPENT BY PERIOD (FILTERED TOTAL)
  double getTotalSpentByPeriod(String period) {
    final filteredTransactions = getTransactionsByPeriod(period);
    return filteredTransactions
        .where((t) => t.isDebit)
        .fold(0.0, (sum, t) => sum + t.amount);
  }

  // GET RECENT TRANSACTIONS BY PERIOD (LAST 10 FROM FILTERED)
  List<Transaction> getRecentTransactionsByPeriod(String period) {
    final filteredTransactions = getTransactionsByPeriod(period);
    return filteredTransactions.take(10).toList();
  }

  // Clear all data (for testing)
  Future<void> clearAllData() async {
    _transactions = [];
    notifyListeners();
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    await prefs.remove('transactions');
  }
}

```

### File 32: add_transaction_screen.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\add_transaction_screen.dart`
**Size:** 4.44 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../widgets/add_transaction/add_transaction_header.dart';
import '../widgets/add_transaction/amount_input_section.dart';
import '../widgets/add_transaction/category_selector.dart';
import '../widgets/add_transaction/date_selector.dart';
import '../widgets/add_transaction/note_input_field.dart';
import '../widgets/add_transaction/numeric_keyboard.dart';
import '../widgets/add_transaction/save_transaction_button.dart';
import 'add_transaction/transaction_logic.dart';
import 'add_transaction/transaction_handlers.dart';

class AddTransactionScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const AddTransactionScreen({super.key});

  @override
  State<AddTransactionScreen> createState() => _AddTransactionScreenState();
}

class _AddTransactionScreenState extends State<AddTransactionScreen> {
  String _amount = '0';
  String _selectedCategory = 'Food';
  DateTime _selectedDate = DateTime.now();
  String _note = '';
  bool _isSaving = false;
  bool _isNoteFieldFocused = false;

  final FocusNode _noteFocusNode = FocusNode();
  late TransactionHandlers _handlers;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _noteFocusNode.addListener(_onNoteFocusChanged);

    _handlers = TransactionHandlers(
      onAmountUpdate: (amount) => setState(() => _amount = amount),
      onCategoryUpdate: (category) => setState(() => _selectedCategory = category),
      onDateUpdate: (date) => setState(() => _selectedDate = date),
      onNoteUpdate: (note) => setState(() => _note = note),
    );
  }

  void _onNoteFocusChanged() {
    setState(() => _isNoteFieldFocused = _noteFocusNode.hasFocus);
  }

  @override
  void dispose() {
    _noteFocusNode.dispose();
    super.dispose();
  }

  Future<void> _onSave() async {
    await TransactionLogic.saveExpense(
      context: context,
      amount: _amount,
      category: _selectedCategory,
      date: _selectedDate,
      note: _note,
      onLoadingChange: (loading) => setState(() => _isSaving = loading),
    );
  }

  void _onClose() {
    TransactionHandlers.showDiscardDialog(context, _amount, _note);
  }

  bool _handleBackPress() {
    if (_isNoteFieldFocused) {
      _noteFocusNode.unfocus();
      return false;
    }
    _onClose();
    return false;
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return PopScope(
      canPop: false,
      onPopInvoked: (didPop) {
        if (!didPop) {
          _handleBackPress();
        }
      },
      child: Scaffold(
        backgroundColor: Colors.white,
        resizeToAvoidBottomInset: true,
        body: SafeArea(
          child: Column(
            children: [
              AddTransactionHeader(onClose: _onClose),
              Expanded(
                child: SingleChildScrollView(
                  padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 24),
                  child: Column(
                    children: [
                      const SizedBox(height: 32),
                      AmountInputSection(amount: _amount),
                      const SizedBox(height: 48),
                      CategorySelector(
                        selectedCategory: _selectedCategory,
                        onCategorySelected: _handlers.handleCategorySelect,
                      ),
                      const SizedBox(height: 40),
                      DateSelector(
                        selectedDate: _selectedDate,
                        onDateSelected: _handlers.handleDateSelect,
                      ),
                      const SizedBox(height: 24),
                      NoteInputField(
                        note: _note,
                        focusNode: _noteFocusNode,
                        onChanged: _handlers.handleNoteChange,
                      ),
                      const SizedBox(height: 32),
                      SaveTransactionButton(
                        onSave: _onSave,
                        isLoading: _isSaving,
                      ),
                      const SizedBox(height: 16),
                    ],
                  ),
                ),
              ),
              if (!_isNoteFieldFocused)
                NumericKeyboard(
                  onNumberTap: (number) => _handlers.handleNumberTap(_amount, number),
                  onBackspace: () => _handlers.handleBackspace(_amount),
                ),
            ],
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../widgets/add_transaction/add_transaction_header.dart';
import '../widgets/add_transaction/amount_input_section.dart';
import '../widgets/add_transaction/category_selector.dart';
import '../widgets/add_transaction/date_selector.dart';
import '../widgets/add_transaction/note_input_field.dart';
import '../widgets/add_transaction/numeric_keyboard.dart';
import '../widgets/add_transaction/save_transaction_button.dart';
import '../models/transaction.dart';
import 'add_transaction/transaction_logic.dart';
import 'add_transaction/transaction_handlers.dart';

class EditTransactionScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  final Transaction transaction;

  const EditTransactionScreen({
    super.key,
    required this.transaction,
  });

  @override
  State<EditTransactionScreen> createState() => _EditTransactionScreenState();
}

class _EditTransactionScreenState extends State<EditTransactionScreen> {
  late String amount;
  late String selectedCategory;
  late DateTime selectedDate;
  late String note;
  bool isSaving = false;
  bool isNoteFieldFocused = false;
  final FocusNode noteFocusNode = FocusNode();
  late TransactionHandlers handlers;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();

    // Pre-fill with existing transaction data
    amount = widget.transaction.amount.toStringAsFixed(2);
    selectedCategory = widget.transaction.category;
    selectedDate = widget.transaction.dateTime;
    note = widget.transaction.merchantName;

    noteFocusNode.addListener(_onNoteFocusChanged);

    handlers = TransactionHandlers(
      onAmountUpdate: (amount) => setState(() => this.amount = amount),
      onCategoryUpdate: (category) => setState(() => selectedCategory = category),
      onDateUpdate: (date) => setState(() => selectedDate = date),
      onNoteUpdate: (note) => setState(() => this.note = note),
    );
  }

  void _onNoteFocusChanged() {
    setState(() {
      isNoteFieldFocused = noteFocusNode.hasFocus;
    });
  }

  @override
  void dispose() {
    noteFocusNode.dispose();
    super.dispose();
  }

  Future<void> _onUpdate() async {
    await TransactionLogic.updateExpense(
      context: context,
      transactionId: widget.transaction.id,
      amount: amount,
      category: selectedCategory,
      date: selectedDate,
      note: note,
      onLoadingChange: (loading) => setState(() => isSaving = loading),
    );
  }

  void _onClose() {
    TransactionHandlers.showDiscardDialog(context, amount, note);
  }

  bool _handleBackPress() {
    if (isNoteFieldFocused) {
      noteFocusNode.unfocus();
      return false;
    }
    _onClose();
    return false;
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return PopScope(
      canPop: false,
      onPopInvoked: (didPop) {
        if (!didPop) _handleBackPress();
      },
      child: Scaffold(
        backgroundColor: Colors.white,
        resizeToAvoidBottomInset: true,
        body: SafeArea(
          child: Column(
            children: [
              // Header with "Edit Expense" title
              Container(
                padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16, vertical: 16),
                child: Row(
                  mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
                  children: [
                    IconButton(
                      onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context),
                      icon: const Icon(Icons.arrow_back),
                      style: IconButton.styleFrom(
                        backgroundColor: Colors.grey.shade100,
                        shape: const CircleBorder(),
                      ),
                    ),
                    const Text(
                      'Edit Expense',
                      style: TextStyle(
                        fontSize: 18,
                        fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                        color: Color(0xFF131615),
                      ),
                    ),
                    IconButton(
                      onPressed: _onClose,
                      icon: const Icon(Icons.close),
                      style: IconButton.styleFrom(
                        backgroundColor: Colors.grey.shade100,
                        shape: const CircleBorder(),
                      ),
                    ),
                  ],
                ),
              ),
              Expanded(
                child: SingleChildScrollView(
                  padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 24),
                  child: Column(
                    children: [
                      const SizedBox(height: 32),
                      AmountInputSection(amount: amount),
                      const SizedBox(height: 48),
                      CategorySelector(
                        selectedCategory: selectedCategory,
                        onCategorySelected: handlers.handleCategorySelect,
                      ),
                      const SizedBox(height: 40),
                      DateSelector(
                        selectedDate: selectedDate,
                        onDateSelected: handlers.handleDateSelect,
                      ),
                      const SizedBox(height: 24),
                      NoteInputField(
                        note: note,
                        focusNode: noteFocusNode,
                        onChanged: handlers.handleNoteChange,
                      ),
                      const SizedBox(height: 32),
                      SaveTransactionButton(
                        onSave: _onUpdate,
                        isLoading: isSaving,
                      ),
                      const SizedBox(height: 16),
                    ],
                  ),
                ),

              if (!isNoteFieldFocused)
                NumericKeyboard(

                  onBackspace: () => handlers.handleBackspace(amount),
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:provider/provider.dart';
import '../providers/expense_provider.dart';
import '../widgets/home/transaction_item.dart';

class HistoryScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const HistoryScreen({super.key});

  @override
  State<HistoryScreen> createState() => _HistoryScreenState();
}

class _HistoryScreenState extends State<HistoryScreen> {
  final TextEditingController _searchController = TextEditingController();
  String _searchQuery = '';

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _searchController.addListener(_onSearchChanged);
  }

  void _onSearchChanged() {
    setState(() {
      _searchQuery = _searchController.text.toLowerCase();
    });
  }

  @override
  void dispose() {
    _searchController.removeListener(_onSearchChanged);
    _searchController.dispose();
    super.dispose();
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: const Color(0xFFF6F8F7),
      appBar: _buildAppBar(),
      body: Column(
        children: [
          _buildSearchBar(),
          Expanded(
            child: Consumer<ExpenseProvider>(
              builder: (context, provider, child) {
                final allTransactions = provider.transactions;

                // Filter transactions based on search query
                final filteredTransactions = _searchQuery.isEmpty
                    ? allTransactions
                    : allTransactions.where((transaction) {
                  final merchantName = transaction.merchantName.toLowerCase();
                  final category = transaction.category.toLowerCase();
                  final amount = transaction.amount.toString();

                  return merchantName.contains(_searchQuery) ||
                      category.contains(_searchQuery) ||
                      amount.contains(_searchQuery);
                }).toList();

                if (filteredTransactions.isEmpty) {
                  return _buildEmptyState();
                }

                return ListView.builder(
                  padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 16),
                  itemCount: filteredTransactions.length,
                  itemBuilder: (context, index) {
                    return TransactionItem(
                      transaction: filteredTransactions[index],
                    );
                  },
                );
              },
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  // ğŸ†• APP BAR WITH BACK BUTTON
  PreferredSizeWidget _buildAppBar() {
    return AppBar(
      backgroundColor: Colors.white,
      elevation: 0,
      leading: IconButton(
        icon: const Icon(Icons.arrow_back, color: Color(0xFF131615)),
        onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context),
      ),
      title: const Text(
        'Transaction History',
        style: TextStyle(
          color: Color(0xFF131615),
          fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
        ),
      ),
      centerTitle: false,
    );
  }

  // ğŸ†• SEARCH BAR
  Widget _buildSearchBar() {
    return Container(
      margin: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: Colors.white,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
        border: Border.all(color: Colors.grey.shade200),
      ),
      child: Row(
        children: [
          const Icon(
            Icons.search,
            color: Color(0xFF6B807A),
            size: 24,
          ),
          const SizedBox(width: 12),
          Expanded(
            child: TextField(
              controller: _searchController,
              decoration: const InputDecoration(
                hintText: 'Search by name, category, amount...',
                hintStyle: TextStyle(
                  color: Color(0xFF6B807A),
                  fontSize: 14,
                ),
                border: InputBorder.none,
                contentPadding: EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 14),
              ),
              style: const TextStyle(
                fontSize: 14,
                color: Color(0xFF131615),
              ),
            ),
          ),
          if (_searchQuery.isNotEmpty)
            IconButton(
              icon: const Icon(
                Icons.clear,
                color: Color(0xFF6B807A),
                size: 20,
              ),
              onPressed: () {
                _searchController.clear();
                setState(() {
                  _searchQuery = '';
                });
              },
            ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  // EMPTY STATE
  Widget _buildEmptyState() {
    return Center(
      child: Column(
        mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
        children: [
          Icon(
            _searchQuery.isEmpty ? Icons.history : Icons.search_off,
            size: 80,
            color: Colors.grey.shade400,
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 16),
          Text(
            _searchQuery.isEmpty
                ? 'No transactions yet'
                : 'No results found',
            style: const TextStyle(
              fontSize: 18,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
              color: Color(0xFF131615),
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 8),
          Text(
            _searchQuery.isEmpty
                ? 'Your transaction history will appear here'
                : 'Try searching with different keywords',
            style: TextStyle(
              fontSize: 14,
              color: Colors.grey.shade600,
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:provider/provider.dart';
import '../widgets/home/home_header.dart';
import '../widgets/home/home_expense_card.dart';
import '../widgets/home/transaction_list.dart';
import '../widgets/home/home_empty_state.dart';
import '../providers/expense_provider.dart';

class HomeBodyContent extends StatelessWidget {
  final String selectedPeriod;
  final VoidCallback onPeriodTap;

  const HomeBodyContent({
    super.key,
    required this.selectedPeriod,
    required this.onPeriodTap,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Consumer<ExpenseProvider>(
      builder: (context, provider, child) {
        // ğŸ†• GET FILTERED DATA BASED ON SELECTED PERIOD
        final filteredTransactions = provider.getRecentTransactionsByPeriod(selectedPeriod);
        final periodTotal = provider.getTotalSpentByPeriod(selectedPeriod);
        final hasTransactions = filteredTransactions.isNotEmpty;

        return Column(
          children: [
            HomeHeader(
              selectedPeriod: selectedPeriod,
              onPeriodTap: onPeriodTap,
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 20),
            HomeExpenseCard(
              totalSpent: periodTotal, // ğŸ†• Shows period-specific total (not all-time)
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 24),
            Expanded(
              child: hasTransactions
                  ? TransactionList(
                transactions: filteredTransactions, // ğŸ†• Shows filtered transactions
                totalExpense: periodTotal,
              )
                  : const HomeEmptyState(),
            ),
          ],
        );
      },
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'home_body_content.dart';
import 'add_transaction_screen.dart';  // âœ… Fixed import path

class HomeScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const HomeScreen({super.key});

  @override
  State<HomeScreen> createState() => _HomeScreenState();
}

class _HomeScreenState extends State<HomeScreen> {
  String selectedPeriod = 'This Month';

  void _showPeriodSelector() {
    showModalBottomSheet(
      context: context,
      backgroundColor: Colors.transparent,
      shape: const RoundedRectangleBorder(
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.vertical(top: Radius.circular(20)),
      ),
      builder: (_) => HomePeriodSheet(
        selectedPeriod: selectedPeriod,
        onPeriodSelected: (period) {
          setState(() {
            selectedPeriod = period;
          });
          Navigator.pop(context);

          // Show confirmation snackbar
          ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
            SnackBar(
              content: Text('Showing $period expenses'),
              duration: const Duration(seconds: 1),
              backgroundColor: const Color(0xFF2F7F68),
            ),
          );
        },
      ),
    );
  }

  void _onAddTransaction() async {
    final result = await Navigator.push(
      context,
      MaterialPageRoute(builder: (_) => const AddTransactionScreen()),
    );

    if (result != null && result is Transaction) {
      // Transaction already saved in provider
      if (mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          SnackBar(
            content: Text('Saved â‚¹${result.amount.toStringAsFixed(0)}'),
            backgroundColor: const Color(0xFF2F7F68),
          ),
        );
      }
    }
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: const Color(0xFFF6F8F7),
      body: SafeArea(
        child: HomeBodyContent(
          selectedPeriod: selectedPeriod,
          onPeriodTap: _showPeriodSelector,
        ),
      ),
      floatingActionButton: HomeFAB(onPressed: _onAddTransaction),
      bottomNavigationBar: const HomeBottomNav(currentIndex: 0),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:provider/provider.dart';
import '../providers/expense_provider.dart';
import '../widgets/insights/insights_app_bar.dart';
import '../widgets/insights/insights_header.dart';
import '../widgets/insights/insights_category_breakdown.dart';
import '../widgets/insights/insights_empty_state.dart';
import '../widgets/insights/insights_data_processor.dart';

class InsightsScreen extends StatelessWidget {
  const InsightsScreen({super.key});

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: const Color(0xFFF6F8F7),
      appBar: const InsightsAppBar(),
      body: Consumer<ExpenseProvider>(
        builder: (context, provider, child) {
          // âœ… CHANGED: Use "This Month" filter like Home Screen
          final filteredTransactions = provider.getTransactionsByPeriod('This Month');

          if (filteredTransactions.isEmpty) {
            return const InsightsEmptyState();
          }

          // Process filtered data
          final dataProcessor = InsightsDataProcessor(filteredTransactions);
          final categoryMap = dataProcessor.getCategoryMap();
          final totalSpent = dataProcessor.getTotalSpent();
          final sortedCategories = dataProcessor.getSortedCategories();

          return SingleChildScrollView(
            padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
            child: Column(
              crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
              children: [
                InsightsHeader(totalSpent: totalSpent),
                const SizedBox(height: 24),
                InsightsCategoryBreakdown(
                  categories: sortedCategories,
                  totalSpent: totalSpent,
                ),
              ],
            ),
          );
        },
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

### File 38: permission_screen.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\permission_screen.dart`
**Size:** 5.34 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:permission_handler/permission_handler.dart';
import '../widgets/permission/permission_illustration.dart';
import '../widgets/permission/permission_header.dart';
import '../widgets/permission/trust_badges.dart';
import '../widgets/permission/permission_buttons.dart';
import '../helpers/sms_permission_helper.dart';
import 'home_screen.dart';

class PermissionScreen extends StatelessWidget {
  const PermissionScreen({super.key});

  /// âœ… REAL SMS PERMISSION REQUEST
  Future<void> _requestPermission(BuildContext context) async {
    try {
      // Show loading
      if (context.mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          const SnackBar(
            content: Text('Requesting SMS permission...'),
            duration: Duration(seconds: 1),
          ),
        );
      }

      // Request permission
      final status = await SmsPermissionHelper.requestPermission();

      // Handle different permission states
      if (context.mounted) {
        if (status.isGranted) {
          // âœ… Permission granted
          ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
            const SnackBar(
              content: Text('âœ“ SMS Permission granted!'),
              backgroundColor: Color(0xFF2F7F68),
              duration: Duration(seconds: 1),
            ),
          );

          // Navigate to Home
          await Future.delayed(const Duration(milliseconds: 500));
          if (context.mounted) {
            Navigator.of(context).pushReplacement(
              MaterialPageRoute(builder: (_) => const HomeScreen()),
            );
          }
        } else if (status.isDenied) {
          // âŒ Permission denied
          ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
            const SnackBar(
              content: Text('SMS permission denied. You can enable it later.'),
              backgroundColor: Colors.orange,
              duration: Duration(seconds: 2),
            ),
          );

          // Still navigate to home
          await Future.delayed(const Duration(milliseconds: 500));
          if (context.mounted) {
            Navigator.of(context).pushReplacement(
              MaterialPageRoute(builder: (_) => const HomeScreen()),
            );
          }
        } else if (status.isPermanentlyDenied) {
          // âš ï¸ Permission permanently denied - show settings dialog
          _showSettingsDialog(context);
        }
      }
    } catch (e) {
      if (context.mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          SnackBar(
            content: Text('Error: $e'),
            backgroundColor: Colors.red,
          ),
        );
      }
    }
  }

  /// Show dialog to open app settings
  void _showSettingsDialog(BuildContext context) {
    showDialog(
      context: context,
      builder: (ctx) => AlertDialog(
        title: const Text('Permission Required'),
        content: const Text(
          'SMS permission is permanently denied. '
              'Please enable it from Settings to track transactions automatically.',
        ),
        shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
        ),
        actions: [
          TextButton(
            onPressed: () {
              Navigator.pop(ctx);
              // Navigate to home anyway
              Navigator.of(context).pushReplacement(
                MaterialPageRoute(builder: (_) => const HomeScreen()),
              );
            },
            child: const Text('Skip'),
          ),
          ElevatedButton(
            onPressed: () async {
              Navigator.pop(ctx);
              // Open app settings
              await openAppSettings();
              // Navigate to home
              if (context.mounted) {
                Navigator.of(context).pushReplacement(
                  MaterialPageRoute(builder: (_) => const HomeScreen()),
                );
              }
            },
            style: ElevatedButton.styleFrom(
              backgroundColor: const Color(0xFF2F7F68),
            ),
            child: const Text('Open Settings'),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  /// Skip permission (navigate directly to home)
  void _skipPermission(BuildContext context) {
    // Navigate to Home Screen directly
    Navigator.of(context).pushReplacement(
      MaterialPageRoute(builder: (_) => const HomeScreen()),
    );
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: Colors.white,
      body: SafeArea(
        child: Column(
          children: [
            const Expanded(
              child: SingleChildScrollView(
                child: Column(
                  children: [
                    SizedBox(height: 48),
                    PermissionIllustration(),
                    SizedBox(height: 32),
                    PermissionHeader(),
                    SizedBox(height: 40),
                    TrustBadges(),
                  ],
                ),
              ),
            ),
            PermissionButtons(
              onAllow: () => _requestPermission(context),
              onSkip: () => _skipPermission(context),
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 8),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}

```

### File 39: splash_screen.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\splash_screen.dart`
**Size:** 6.55 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'dart:async';
import '../constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../constants/app_strings.dart';
import 'welcome_screen.dart';

class SplashScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const SplashScreen({super.key});

  @override
  State<SplashScreen> createState() => _SplashScreenState();
}

class _SplashScreenState extends State<SplashScreen>
    with SingleTickerProviderStateMixin {
  late AnimationController _controller;
  late Animation<double> _fadeAnimation;
  late Animation<double> _scaleAnimation;
  double _progress = 0.0;
  Timer? _progressTimer;
  Timer? _navigationTimer;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();

    _controller = AnimationController(
      duration: const Duration(milliseconds: 1500),
      vsync: this,
    );

    _fadeAnimation = Tween<double>(begin: 0.0, end: 1.0).animate(
      CurvedAnimation(parent: _controller, curve: Curves.easeIn),
    );

    _scaleAnimation = Tween<double>(begin: 0.8, end: 1.0).animate(
      CurvedAnimation(parent: _controller, curve: Curves.easeOutBack),
    );

    _controller.forward();
    _startProgress();
    _navigateToWelcome();
  }

  void _startProgress() {
    _progressTimer = Timer.periodic(const Duration(milliseconds: 50), (timer) {
      if (mounted) {
        if (_progress >= 1.0) {
          timer.cancel();
        } else {
          setState(() {
            _progress += 0.02;
          });
        }
      } else {
        timer.cancel();
      }
    });
  }

  void _navigateToWelcome() {
    _navigationTimer = Timer(const Duration(seconds: 3), () {
      if (mounted) {
        Navigator.of(context).pushReplacement(
          MaterialPageRoute(builder: (_) => const WelcomeScreen()),
        );
      }
    });
  }

  @override
  void dispose() {
    _progressTimer?.cancel();
    _navigationTimer?.cancel();
    _controller.dispose();
    super.dispose();
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      body: Container(
        decoration: const BoxDecoration(
          gradient: LinearGradient(
            begin: Alignment.topCenter,
            end: Alignment.bottomCenter,
            colors: [
              AppColors.primary,
              AppColors.background,
            ],
          ),
        ),
        child: Stack(
          children: [
            _buildDecorativeCircles(),

    );

            mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,

                      Icon(
                        Icons.trending_up,
                        size: 60,

                      ),
                      const Positioned(
                        bottom: 15,
                        child: Text(
                          'â‚¹',
                          style: TextStyle(
                            fontSize: 28,

                          ),
```

### File 41: transaction_handlers.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\add_transaction\transaction_handlers.dart`
**Size:** 3.32 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'transaction_validation.dart';

class TransactionHandlers {
  final Function(String) onAmountUpdate;
  final Function(String) onCategoryUpdate;
  final Function(DateTime) onDateUpdate;
  final Function(String) onNoteUpdate;

  TransactionHandlers({
    required this.onAmountUpdate,
    required this.onCategoryUpdate,
    required this.onDateUpdate,
    required this.onNoteUpdate,
  });

  void handleNumberTap(String currentAmount, String number) {
    String newAmount = currentAmount;

    if (number == '.') {
      if (currentAmount.contains('.')) return;
      if (currentAmount == '0') {
        onAmountUpdate('0.');
        return;
      }
    }

    if (currentAmount == '0' && number != '.') {
      newAmount = number;
    } else if (currentAmount.length < 10) {
      final testAmount = currentAmount + number;
      if (TransactionValidation.isValidDecimal(testAmount)) {
        newAmount = testAmount;
      }
    }

    onAmountUpdate(newAmount);
  }

  void handleBackspace(String currentAmount) {
    if (currentAmount.length > 1) {
      onAmountUpdate(currentAmount.substring(0, currentAmount.length - 1));
    } else {
      onAmountUpdate('0');
    }
  }

  void handleCategorySelect(String category) {
    onCategoryUpdate(category);
  }

  void handleDateSelect(DateTime date) {
    onDateUpdate(date);
  }

  void handleNoteChange(String note) {
    onNoteUpdate(note);
  }

  static void showError(BuildContext context, String message) {
    ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
      SnackBar(
        content: Text(message),
        backgroundColor: Colors.red.shade600,
        behavior: SnackBarBehavior.floating,
        margin: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
        shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(8),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  static void showSuccess(BuildContext context, String message) {
    ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
      SnackBar(
        content: Text(message),
        backgroundColor: const Color(0xFF2F7F68),
        behavior: SnackBarBehavior.floating,
        margin: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
        shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(8),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  static void showDiscardDialog(
      BuildContext context,
      String amount,
      String note,
      ) {
    if (amount != '0' || note.isNotEmpty) {
      showDialog(
        context: context,
        builder: (ctx) => AlertDialog(
          title: const Text('Discard changes?'),
          content: const Text('Your expense will not be saved.'),
          shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(
            borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
          ),
          actions: [
            TextButton(
              onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(ctx),
              child: const Text('Cancel'),
            ),
            TextButton(
              onPressed: () {
                Navigator.pop(ctx);
                Navigator.pop(context);
              },
              child: const Text(
                'Discard',
                style: TextStyle(color: Colors.red),
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      );
    } else {
      Navigator.pop(context);
    }
  }
}

```

### File 42: transaction_logic.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\add_transaction\transaction_logic.dart`
**Size:** 3.79 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:provider/provider.dart';
import '../../models/transaction.dart';
import '../../providers/expense_provider.dart';
import 'transaction_validation.dart';
import 'transaction_handlers.dart';

class TransactionLogic {
  // Existing saveExpense method (keep as is)
  static Future<void> saveExpense({
    required BuildContext context,
    required String amount,
    required String category,
    required DateTime date,
    required String note,
    required Function(bool) onLoadingChange,
  }) async {
    // Validation
    final amountError = TransactionValidation.validateAmount(amount);
    if (amountError != null) {
      TransactionHandlers.showError(context, amountError);
      return;
    }

    final categoryError = TransactionValidation.validateCategory(category);
    if (categoryError != null) {
      TransactionHandlers.showError(context, categoryError);
      return;
    }

    onLoadingChange(true);

    try {
      // Create transaction object
      final transaction = Transaction(
        id: DateTime.now().millisecondsSinceEpoch.toString(),
        merchantName: note.trim().isEmpty ? category : note.trim(),
        amount: double.parse(amount),
        dateTime: date,
        category: category,
        isDebit: true,
      );

      // Save to provider
      final provider = Provider.of<ExpenseProvider>(context, listen: false);
      provider.addExpense(transaction);

      // Small delay for UX
      await Future.delayed(const Duration(milliseconds: 300));

      if (context.mounted) {
        // Show success message
        TransactionHandlers.showSuccess(
          context,
          'Expense saved: â‚¹$amount',
        );

        // Close screen
        await Future.delayed(const Duration(milliseconds: 500));
        Navigator.pop(context, true);
      }
    } catch (e) {
      TransactionHandlers.showError(context, 'Failed to save expense');
    }

    onLoadingChange(false);
  }

  // ğŸ†• UPDATE EXPENSE METHOD
  static Future<void> updateExpense({
    required BuildContext context,
    required String transactionId,
    required String amount,
    required String category,
    required DateTime date,
    required String note,
    required Function(bool) onLoadingChange,
  }) async {
    // Validation
    final amountError = TransactionValidation.validateAmount(amount);
    if (amountError != null) {
      TransactionHandlers.showError(context, amountError);
      return;
    }

    final categoryError = TransactionValidation.validateCategory(category);
    if (categoryError != null) {
      TransactionHandlers.showError(context, categoryError);
      return;
    }

    onLoadingChange(true);

    try {
      // Create updated transaction object (keeping same ID)
      final updatedTransaction = Transaction(
        id: transactionId, // Keep original ID
        merchantName: note.trim().isEmpty ? category : note.trim(),
        amount: double.parse(amount),
        dateTime: date,
        category: category,
        isDebit: true,
      );

      // Update in provider
      final provider = Provider.of<ExpenseProvider>(context, listen: false);
      provider.updateExpense(updatedTransaction);

      // Small delay for UX
      await Future.delayed(const Duration(milliseconds: 300));

      if (context.mounted) {
        // Show success message
        TransactionHandlers.showSuccess(
          context,
          'Transaction updated',
        );

        // Close screen
        await Future.delayed(const Duration(milliseconds: 500));
        Navigator.pop(context, true);
      }
    } catch (e) {
      TransactionHandlers.showError(context, 'Failed to update transaction');
    }

    onLoadingChange(false);
  }
}
```

### File 43: transaction_validation.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\add_transaction\transaction_validation.dart`
**Size:** 868.00 Bytes

```dart
class TransactionValidation {
  static String? validateAmount(String amount) {
    if (amount.isEmpty || amount == '0' || amount == '0.') {
      return 'Please enter amount';
    }

    final value = double.tryParse(amount);
    if (value == null) {
      return 'Invalid amount';
    }

    if (value <= 0) {
      return 'Amount must be greater than 0';
    }

    if (value > 1000000) {
      return 'Amount too large (max â‚¹10,00,000)';
    }

    return null;
  }

  static String? validateCategory(String category) {
    if (category.isEmpty) {
      return 'Please select a category';
    }
    return null;
  }

  static bool isValidDecimal(String amount) {
    final parts = amount.split('.');
    if (parts.length > 2) return false;
    if (parts.length == 2 && parts[1].length > 2) return false;
    return true;
  }
}

```

### File 45: profile_export_logic.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\profile\profile_export_logic.dart`
**Size:** 4.41 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:provider/provider.dart';
import 'package:share_plus/share_plus.dart';
import '../../providers/expense_provider.dart';
import '../../helpers/csv_exporter.dart';

class ProfileExportLogic {
  // Export Data to CSV
  static Future<void> exportData(BuildContext context) async {
    try {
      final provider = Provider.of<ExpenseProvider>(context, listen: false);
      final transactions = provider.transactions;

      if (transactions.isEmpty) {
        if (context.mounted) {
          ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
            const SnackBar(
              content: Text('No transactions to export'),
              backgroundColor: Colors.orange,
            ),
          );
        }
        return;
      }

      // Show loading
      if (context.mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          const SnackBar(
            content: Text('Exporting data...'),
            duration: Duration(seconds: 1),
          ),
        );
      }

      // Generate and save CSV
      final file = await CsvExporter.saveCsv(transactions);

      // Show success with share option
      if (context.mounted) {
        final result = await showDialog<bool>(
          context: context,
          builder: (context) => AlertDialog(
            title: const Text('Export Successful'),
            content: Text(
              '${transactions.length} transactions exported to\n${file.path}',
            ),
            actions: [
              TextButton(
                onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, false),
                child: const Text('OK'),
              ),
              ElevatedButton(
                onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, true),
                style: ElevatedButton.styleFrom(
                  backgroundColor: const Color(0xFF2F7F68),
                ),
                child: const Text('Share'),
              ),
            ],
          ),
        );

        // Share file if requested
        if (result == true) {
          await Share.shareXFiles(
            [XFile(file.path)],
            text: 'Spendly Transaction Export',
          );
        }
      }
    } catch (e) {
      if (context.mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          SnackBar(
            content: Text('Export failed: $e'),
            backgroundColor: Colors.red,
          ),
        );
      }
    }
  }

  // Generate Monthly Report
  static Future<void> generateMonthlyReport(BuildContext context) async {
    try {
      final provider = Provider.of<ExpenseProvider>(context, listen: false);
      final transactions = provider.transactions;

      if (transactions.isEmpty) {
        if (context.mounted) {
          ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
            const SnackBar(
              content: Text('No transactions for report'),
              backgroundColor: Colors.orange,
            ),
          );
        }
        return;
      }

      final summary = CsvExporter.generateMonthlySummary(transactions);

      if (context.mounted) {
        showDialog(
          context: context,
          builder: (context) => AlertDialog(
            title: const Text('Monthly Report'),
            content: SingleChildScrollView(
              child: Text(
                summary,
                style: const TextStyle(fontFamily: 'monospace'),
              ),
            ),
            actions: [
              TextButton(
                onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context),
                child: const Text('Close'),
              ),
              ElevatedButton(
                onPressed: () {
                  Navigator.pop(context);
                  Share.share(
                    summary,
                    subject: 'Spendly Monthly Report',
                  );
                },
                style: ElevatedButton.styleFrom(
                  backgroundColor: const Color(0xFF2F7F68),
                ),
                child: const Text('Share'),
              ),
            ],
          ),
        );
      }
    } catch (e) {
      if (context.mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          SnackBar(
            content: Text('Report generation failed: $e'),
            backgroundColor: Colors.red,
          ),
        );
      }
    }
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

class ProfileWidgets {
  // Profile Header Widget
  static Widget buildProfileHeader() {
    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(20),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: Colors.white,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
      ),
      child: Row(
        children: [
          // Profile Avatar
          Container(
            width: 60,
            height: 60,
            decoration: const BoxDecoration(
              color: Color(0xFF2F7F68),
              shape: BoxShape.circle,
            ),
            child: const Icon(
              Icons.person,
              size: 32,
              color: Colors.white,
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(width: 16),

          // Profile Info
          Column(
            crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
            children: [
              const Text(
                'Spendly User',
                style: TextStyle(
                  fontSize: 18,
                  fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                ),
              ),
              const SizedBox(height: 4),
              Text(
                'Tracking expenses since 2026',
                style: TextStyle(
                  fontSize: 12,
                  color: Colors.grey.shade600,
                ),
              ),
            ],
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  // Section Title
  static Widget buildSectionTitle(String title) {
    return Padding(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.only(left: 4, bottom: 8, top: 8),
      child: Text(
        title,
        style: TextStyle(
          fontSize: 14,
          fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
          color: Colors.grey.shade600,
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  // Settings Tile Widget
  static Widget buildSettingsTile({
    required IconData icon,
    required String title,
    String? subtitle,
    required VoidCallback onTap,
  }) {
    return Container(
      margin: const EdgeInsets.only(bottom: 8),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: Colors.white,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
      ),
      child: ListTile(
        leading: Icon(
          icon,
          color: const Color(0xFF2F7F68),
        ),
        title: Text(title),
        subtitle: subtitle != null
            ? Text(
          subtitle,
          style: TextStyle(
            fontSize: 12,
            color: Colors.grey.shade600,
          ),
        )
            : null,
        trailing: const Icon(
          Icons.chevron_right,
          color: Colors.grey,
        ),
        onTap: onTap,
      ),
    );
```

```dart
class AddTransactionHeader extends StatelessWidget {

        mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,

        ],
      ),
    );

    return IconButton(
      onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context),
      icon: const Icon(Icons.arrow_back, size: 24),
      style: IconButton.styleFrom(
        backgroundColor: Colors.grey.shade100,
        shape: const CircleBorder(),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildCloseButton() {
    return IconButton(
      onPressed: onClose,
      icon: const Icon(Icons.close, size: 24),
      style: IconButton.styleFrom(
        backgroundColor: Colors.grey.shade100,
        shape: const CircleBorder(),
      ),
    );
```

**Size:** 2.38 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

class CategorySelector extends StatelessWidget {
  final String selectedCategory;
  final Function(String) onCategorySelected;

  const CategorySelector({
    super.key,
    required this.selectedCategory,
    required this.onCategorySelected,
  });

  static const categories = [
    {'name': 'Food', 'emoji': 'ğŸ”', 'color': Color(0xFFF97316)},
    {'name': 'Travel', 'emoji': 'ğŸš•', 'color': Color(0xFF3B82F6)},
    {'name': 'Shopping', 'emoji': 'ğŸ›’', 'color': Color(0xFFA855F7)},
    {'name': 'Bills', 'emoji': 'ğŸ’¡', 'color': Color(0xFFEAB308)},
    {'name': 'Entertainment', 'emoji': 'ğŸ¬', 'color': Color(0xFFEC4899)},
    {'name': 'Health', 'emoji': 'ğŸ’Š', 'color': Color(0xFFEF4444)},
    {'name': 'Others', 'emoji': 'ğŸ“Œ', 'color': Color(0xFF6B7280)},
  ];

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return SingleChildScrollView(
      scrollDirection: Axis.horizontal,
      child: Row(
        children: categories.map((category) {
          return Padding(
            padding: const EdgeInsets.only(right: 12),
            child: _buildCategoryChip(category),
          );
        }).toList(),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildCategoryChip(Map<String, dynamic> category) {
    final isSelected = category['name'] == selectedCategory;
    final color = category['color'] as Color;

    return InkWell(
      onTap: () => onCategorySelected(category['name'] as String),
      borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(24),
      child: Container(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 20, vertical: 10),
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          color: isSelected ? color : color.withOpacity(0.1),
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(24),
          border: Border.all(
            color: isSelected ? color : color.withOpacity(0.3),
          ),
        ),
        child: Row(
          mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
          children: [
            Text(category['emoji'] as String, style: const TextStyle(fontSize: 18)),
            const SizedBox(width: 8),
            Text(
              category['name'] as String,
              style: TextStyle(
                fontSize: 14,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
                color: isSelected ? Colors.white : color,
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

### File 52: date_selector.dart
**Path:** `lib\widgets\add_transaction\date_selector.dart`
**Size:** 3.44 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
// import 'package:intl/intl.dart';

class DateSelector extends StatelessWidget {
  final DateTime selectedDate;
  final Function(DateTime) onDateSelected;

  const DateSelector({
    super.key,
    required this.selectedDate,
    required this.onDateSelected,
  });

  String _formatDate(DateTime date) {
    final now = DateTime.now();
    final today = DateTime(now.year, now.month, now.day);
    final yesterday = today.subtract(const Duration(days: 1));
    final selected = DateTime(date.year, date.month, date.day);

    if (selected == today) {
      return 'Today';
    } else if (selected == yesterday) {
      return 'Yesterday';
    } else {
      // Temporary simple format without intl package
      return '${date.day}/${date.month}/${date.year}';

      // âœ… Uncomment below after flutter pub get
      // return DateFormat('dd MMM yyyy').format(date);
    }
  }

  Future<void> _pickDate(BuildContext context) async {
    final picked = await showDatePicker(
      context: context,
      initialDate: selectedDate,
      firstDate: DateTime(2020),
      lastDate: DateTime.now(),
      builder: (context, child) {
        return Theme(
          data: Theme.of(context).copyWith(
            colorScheme: const ColorScheme.light(
              primary: Color(0xFF2F7F68),
              onPrimary: Colors.white,
              onSurface: Colors.black,
            ),
          ),
          child: child!,
        );
      },
    );

    if (picked != null && picked != selectedDate) {
      onDateSelected(picked);
    }
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return InkWell(
      onTap: () => _pickDate(context),
      borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
      child: Container(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          color: Colors.grey.shade50,
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
          border: Border.all(color: Colors.grey.shade200),
        ),
        child: Row(
          children: [
            Container(
              padding: const EdgeInsets.all(10),
              decoration: BoxDecoration(
                color: const Color(0xFF2F7F68).withValues(alpha: 0.1),
                borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
              ),
              child: const Icon(
                Icons.calendar_today,
                color: Color(0xFF2F7F68),
                size: 20,
              ),
            ),
            const SizedBox(width: 16),
            Expanded(
              child: Column(
                crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
                children: [
                  Text(
                    'Date',
                    style: TextStyle(
                      fontSize: 12,
                      color: Colors.grey.shade600,
                    ),
                  ),
                  const SizedBox(height: 4),
                  Text(
                    _formatDate(selectedDate),
                    style: const TextStyle(
                      fontSize: 16,
                      fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
                    ),
                  ),
                ],
              ),
            ),
            Icon(
              Icons.arrow_forward_ios,
              size: 16,
              color: Colors.grey.shade400,
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
              ),
              style: const TextStyle(fontSize: 16),
              maxLength: 50,
              buildCounter: (context, {required currentLength, required isFocused, maxLength}) => null,
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
```

### File 54: numeric_keyboard.dart
**Path:** `lib\widgets\add_transaction\numeric_keyboard.dart`
**Size:** 3.01 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

class NumericKeyboard extends StatelessWidget {
  final Function(String) onNumberTap;
  final VoidCallback onBackspace;

  const NumericKeyboard({
    super.key,
    required this.onNumberTap,
    required this.onBackspace,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(8),
      color: Colors.grey.shade100,
      child: Column(
        mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
        children: [
          _buildRow(['1', '2', '3']),
          const SizedBox(height: 8),
          _buildRow(['4', '5', '6']),
          const SizedBox(height: 8),
          _buildRow(['7', '8', '9']),
          const SizedBox(height: 8),
          _buildBottomRow(),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildRow(List<String> numbers) {
    return Row(
      children: numbers.map((number) {
        return Expanded(
          child: Padding(
            padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 4),
            child: _buildKey(number),
          ),
        );
      }).toList(),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildBottomRow() {
    return Row(
      children: [
        Expanded(
          child: Padding(
            padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 4),
            child: _buildKey('.'),
          ),
        ),
        Expanded(
          child: Padding(
            padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 4),
            child: _buildKey('0'),
          ),
        ),
        Expanded(
          child: Padding(
            padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 4),
            child: _buildBackspaceKey(),
          ),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _buildKey(String number) {
    return Material(
      color: Colors.white,
      borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
      child: InkWell(
        onTap: () => onNumberTap(number),
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
        child: Container(
          height: 52,
          decoration: BoxDecoration(
            borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
            boxShadow: [
              BoxShadow(
                color: Colors.black.withOpacity(0.05),
                blurRadius: 4,
              ),
            ],
          ),
          child: Center(
            child: Text(
              number,
              style: const TextStyle(
                fontSize: 24,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
              ),
            ),
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildBackspaceKey() {
    return Material(
      color: Colors.transparent,
      child: InkWell(
        onTap: onBackspace,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
        child: Container(
          height: 52,
          child: const Center(
            child: Icon(
              Icons.backspace_outlined,
              size: 26,
              color: Colors.black87,
            ),
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}

```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

class SaveTransactionButton extends StatelessWidget {
  final VoidCallback onSave;
  final bool isLoading;

  const SaveTransactionButton({
    super.key,
    required this.onSave,
    this.isLoading = false,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return SizedBox(
      width: double.infinity,
      height: 56,
      child: ElevatedButton(
        onPressed: isLoading ? null : onSave,
        style: ElevatedButton.styleFrom(
          backgroundColor: const Color(0xFF2F7F68),
          disabledBackgroundColor: const Color(0xFF2F7F68).withOpacity(0.5),
          shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(
            borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(28),
          ),
          elevation: 6,
        ),
        child: isLoading
            ? const SizedBox(
          width: 24,
          height: 24,
          child: CircularProgressIndicator(
            strokeWidth: 2,
            valueColor: AlwaysStoppedAnimation<Color>(Colors.white),
          ),
        )
            : const Text(
          'Save Expense',
          style: TextStyle(
            fontSize: 18,
            fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
            color: Colors.white,
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../constants/app_colors.dart';

class BottomNavBar extends StatelessWidget {
  final int currentIndex;

  const BottomNavBar({
    super.key,
    required this.currentIndex,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Container(
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: Colors.white,
        border: Border(
          top: BorderSide(color: Colors.grey.shade200),
        ),
      ),
      child: SafeArea(
        child: Padding(
          padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 8),
          child: Row(
            mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceAround,
            children: [
              _buildNavItem(0, Icons.home, 'Home', filled: true),
              _buildNavItem(1, Icons.receipt, 'History'),
              _buildNavItem(2, Icons.analytics, 'Insights'),
              _buildNavItem(3, Icons.person, 'Profile'),
            ],
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildNavItem(int index, IconData icon, String label, {bool filled = false}) {
    final isSelected = index == currentIndex;

    return Column(
      mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
      children: [
        Icon(
          icon,
          color: isSelected ? AppColors.primary : const Color(0xFF6B807A),
          size: 24,
          fill: (filled && isSelected) ? 1.0 : 0.0,
        ),
        const SizedBox(height: 4),
        Text(
          label,
          style: TextStyle(
            fontSize: 12,
            fontWeight: isSelected ? FontWeight.bold : FontWeight.w500,
            color: isSelected ? AppColors.primary : const Color(0xFF6B807A),
          ),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }
}
```
